1.

Enter only data

suitable for release in case of need, without jeopardizing CS sources.

methods or operations. Only substantiated, reliable information may be recorded.

para 8, in the Instructiong under Item & concerning the abbreviations of organization?

3. Sample standardized entries for several items for guideline purposes follow:

(1) Jorge RAMIRE?, Clauro: (3) Il January 1917; (4) Bogota, Colombia; (5) Boliva:

(6) Teacher; (7) Residing al 12 venida Espana, La Paz, Bólivia, as of Februar.

1965. See Section 11, para 8, oi Instruciions for detailed guidance on completing

4. A precise record of source and documentation data for the information entries muss.

be maintained.

The researcher may simply enter the required source data for each

item, referencing the appropriate item nurber under Entry Nos. column.

Or, if he

prefers, he may place a footnote numbes, beginning wich (l), encircled or in

parentheses, after the pertinene entry or bit of information. Record the footnote

number under the Entry Nos, column wth pertinent source and documentation dala.

Hence the same footnote number may be used repeatedly after any information

untrios where suurce, document, etc, are the dame.

sypis muss be cautioned not to include the footnote relerence numbera.

iurner ul the lorm. The Worksheet must be lastoned and retained insido the lets

specific dispatch or cable:

c. "Action" - initials of the analyst or officer responsible for the specific step.

together with the date of action completed;

d:

"Validated:' - initials of the responsible reviewing officer and date of such

review action.

Validation must always be recorded for items 6 and 7, which

entails the approval of the final clean copy text of a listing for incorporation

in the SWL Country Notebook:

e: Items 10, ll, and 12 are reserved for possible future use:

Under the item

Periodic Review", the dale when the next periodic review of the

SWL listing will be made should appear immediately after the k. It is recommended

that the officer responsible for the maintenance of the SWU for a specific country

enter this date on the desk copy of the 201 print-out of all SWi personalities to use

as a reminder. It is also recommended that the station copy of the SwL 201 print-

out list carry, for each name, a 'preliminary resiew" date at least one month

earlier than the HQS review date.

On the basis of this reminder the station can

then undertake a final cansassing of available sources to bring entries on the

individual up to date and transmit the results to HQs just prior to the periodic

review in HQs.
